"use strict";
 
var resources = require('./resources'),
    util = require('./util');
 
function BuildInfo(buildNumber, status, cordovaVersion, buildCommand, configuration, options, buildDir, serverDir) {
    this.buildNumber = buildNumber;
    this.status = status;
    this.cordovaVersion = cordovaVersion;
    this.buildCommand = buildCommand;
    this.configuration = configuration;
    this.options = options;
    this.buildDir = buildDir;
    this.serverDir = serverDir,
    this.submissionTime = new Date();
    this.changeList = null;
};
 
BuildInfo.prototype.updateStatus = function(status, messageId, messageArgs) {
    this.status = status;
    this.messageId = messageId;
    if (arguments.length > 2) {
        this.messageArgs = util.getOptionalArgsArrayFromFunctionCall(arguments, 2);
    } 
    this.statusTime = new Date();
};
 
BuildInfo.prototype.localize = function(req) {
    if (this.messageId) {
        this.message = resources.getString(req, this.messageId, this.messageArgs);
    } else {
        this.message = resources.getString(req, 'Build-'+this.status);
    }
    return this;
};
 
module.exports.BuildInfo = BuildInfo;
module.exports.createNewBuildInfoFromDataObject = function(buildInfoData) {
    var bi = new BuildInfo();
    Object.keys(buildInfoData).forEach(function(k) { bi[k] = buildInfoData[k]; });
    return bi;
};
 
module.exports.UPLOADING = 'uploading';
module.exports.UPLOADED = 'uploaded';
module.exports.EXTRACTED = 'extracted';
module.exports.INVALID = 'invalid';
module.exports.BUILDING = 'building';
module.exports.COMPLETE = 'complete';
module.exports.EMULATED = 'emulated';
module.exports.RUNNING = 'running';
module.exports.INSTALLED = 'installed';
module.exports.DOWNLOADED = 'downloaded';
module.exports.DELETED = 'deleted';
module.exports.ERROR = 'error';

"use strict";
 
var fs = require('fs'),
    path = require('path');
 
var BuildLogger = exports = module.exports = function BuildLogger() {
    this.stream = null;
};
 
BuildLogger.prototype = {
    begin: function(buildDir, logFileName, buildProcess) {
        var pathToBuildLog = path.join(buildDir, logFileName);
        this.stream = fs.createWriteStream(pathToBuildLog);
        console.info('Opened build log file %s', pathToBuildLog);
        this.stream.on('error', function(err) {
            console.error('Error from writing to stream at %s: %s', pathToBuildLog, err);
        });
        var me = this;
        buildProcess.stdout.on('data', function(data) {
            me.log(data);
        });
        buildProcess.stderr.on('data', function(data) {
            me.log(data);
        });
    },
 
    end: function() {
        if (this.stream !== null) {
            this.stream.end();
        }
        this.stream = null;
    },
 
    log: function(message) {
        this.stream.write(message);
    }
};

"use strict";
 
var et = require('elementtree'),
    path = require('path'),
	util = require('./util'),
	unorm = require('unorm');
 
function CordovaConfig(configXmlPath) {
    var contents = util.readFileContentsSync(configXmlPath, 'utf-8');
    this.doc = new et.ElementTree(et.XML(contents));
}
 
function getNodeTextSafe(doc, nodeName) {
    var el = doc.find(nodeName);
    return el && el.text && el.text.trim().normalize();
}
 
function getRootAttributeValueSafe(doc, attribName) {
    var el = doc.getroot();
    return el && el.attrib && el.attrib[attribName];
}
 
function getPreferences(doc) {
    var data = {};
    
    var preferences = doc.findall('preference');
    preferences.forEach(function (preference) {
        data[preference.attrib['name']] = preference.attrib['value'];
    });
    
    return data;
}
 
CordovaConfig.prototype = {
    id: function() {
        return this.doc.getroot().attrib.id;
    },
    name: function() {
        return getNodeTextSafe(this.doc, 'name');
    },
    version: function() {
        return getRootAttributeValueSafe(this.doc, 'version');
    },
    preferences: function() {
	    return getPreferences(this.doc);
    },
};
 
module.exports = CordovaConfig;

"use strict";
 
var exec = require('child_process').exec
  , Q = require('q')
  , util = require('./util')
  , res = require('./resources');
 
var installer = exports = module.exports = {};
 
installer.install = function (ipaPath) {
    var quoteSafeIpaPath = util.quotesAroundIfNecessary(ipaPath);
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    exec('ideviceinstaller -i ' + quoteSafeIpaPath, function (err, stdout, stderr) {
		if (stdout.indexOf("ApplicationVerificationFailed") > -1) {
			deferred.reject({ reason: 'ProvisioningFailed' });
		} else if (err) {
			if (err.message.indexOf("No iOS device found, is it plugged in?") > -1) {
				deferred.reject({ reason: 'InstallFailNoDevice' });
			} else {
				deferred.reject(err);
			}
        } else if (stderr.toLowerCase().indexOf("error") > -1) {
            deferred.reject(stderr);
        } else {
            deferred.resolve(stdout);
        }
    });
    return deferred.promise;
};

"use strict";
 
var exec = require('child_process').exec
  , Q = require('q')
  , pl = require('plist-with-patches')
  , util = require('./util')
  , net = require('net')
  , fs = require('fs');
 
var runner = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var promiseExec = Q.denodeify(exec);
 
var getDiskImageInfo = function () {
    // Attempt to find the OS version of the iDevice, e.g. 7.1
    var versionInfo = promiseExec("ideviceinfo -s -k ProductVersion").then(function (args) {
        var stdout = args[0];
        return stdout.trim().substring(0, 3); // Versions for DeveloperDiskImage seem to be X.Y, while some device versions are X.Y.Z
        // NOTE: This will almost certainly be wrong in the next few years, once we hit version 10.0 
    }, function (err) {
        throw new Error("Can't get device info");
    });
    
    // Attempt to find the path where developer resources exist.
    var pathInfo = promiseExec("xcrun -sdk iphoneos --show-sdk-platform-path").then(function (args) {
        var sdkpath = args[0].trim();
        return sdkpath;
    });
    
    // Attempt to find the developer disk image for the appropriate 
    return Q.all([versionInfo, pathInfo]).spread(function (version, sdkpath) {
        var spaceSafeName = util.quotesAroundIfNecessary(sdkpath);
        return promiseExec('find ' + spaceSafeName + ' -path "*' + version + '*" -name "DeveloperDiskImage.dmg"');
    });
}
 
var mountDeveloperImage = function () {
    return getDiskImageInfo().then(function (args) {
        var findStdOut = args[0];
        var candidate = findStdOut.split("\n")[0];
        var dmgPath = candidate.trim();
        if (dmgPath == "") {
            throw new Error("Unable to find DeveloperDiskImage.dmg");
        }
        var quoteSafeDmgPath = util.quotesAroundIfNecessary(dmgPath);
        var deferred = Q.defer();
        exec('ideviceimagemounter ' + quoteSafeDmgPath, function (err, stdout, stderr) {
            if (err) {
                if (stdout.indexOf("Error:") > -1) {
                    deferred.resolve('Failed; may already be mounted?');
                } else if (stdout.indexOf('No device found, is it plugged in?') > -1) {
                    deferred.reject(new Error("No Device Attached"));
                }
            } else {
                deferred.resolve(stdout);
            }
        });
        return deferred.promise;
    });
}
 
var proxyInstance = null;
var webProxyInstance = null;
 
runner.shutdown = function () {
    if (proxyInstance) {
        console.info("Shutting down native debug proxy...");
        proxyInstance.kill('SIGHUP');
        proxyInstance = null;
    }
    if (webProxyInstance) {
        console.info("Shutting down web debug proxy...");
        webProxyInstance.kill();
        webProxyInstance = null;
    }
}
 
// Attempt to start the debug server proxy listening on a given port. Returns the executable, so it can be stopped later if necessary.
runner.startDebugProxy = function (portNumber) {
    if (proxyInstance != null) {
        proxyInstance.kill('SIGHUP'); // idevicedebugserver does not exit from SIGTERM
        proxyInstance = null;
    }
    return mountDeveloperImage().then(function () {
        proxyInstance = exec('idevicedebugserverproxy ' + portNumber);
        return proxyInstance;
    });
}
 
runner.startiOSWebkitDebugProxy = function (devicePortNumber, portRangeMin, portRangeMax) {
    if (webProxyInstance != null) {
        webProxyInstance.kill(); // sigterm works fine and allows for a graceful exit.
        webProxyInstance = null;
    }
    var commandString = 'ios_webkit_debug_proxy -c null:' + devicePortNumber + ",:" + portRangeMin + "-" + portRangeMax;
    console.info("Running command '"+commandString+"'");
    webProxyInstance = exec(commandString);
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    setTimeout(function () {
        if (!webProxyInstance) {
            deferred.reject('WebkitProxyFailed');
        }
        if (webProxyInstance.exitCode) {
            deferred.reject('WebkitProxyFailed');
        }
        deferred.resolve(webProxyInstance);
    }, 250);
    return deferred.promise;
}
 
runner.encodePath = function (packagePath) {
    // Encode the path by converting each character value to hex
    var encodedPath = "";
    for (var i = 0; i < packagePath.length; ++i) {
        var c = packagePath[i];
        encodedPath += charToHex(c);
    }
    return encodedPath;
}
 
runner.startAppViaDebugger = function (portNumber) {
    return function (packagePath) {
        var encodedPath = runner.encodePath(packagePath);
        
        // We need to send 3 messages to the proxy, waiting for responses between each message:
        
        // A(length of encoded path),0,(encoded path)
        // Hc0
        // c
        
        // We expect a '+' for each message sent, followed by a $OK#9a to indicate that everything has worked.
        
        // For more info, see http://www.opensource.apple.com/source/lldb/lldb-167.2/docs/lldb-gdb-remote.txt
        
        var socket = new net.Socket();
        socket.initState = 0;
        socket.endStatus = null;
        socket.endSignal = null;
        
        var deferred1 = Q.defer();
        var deferred2 = Q.defer();
        var deferred3 = Q.defer();
        
        socket.on("data", function (data) {
            data = data.toString();
            while (data[0] == '+') { data = data.substring(1); }
            // Acknowledge any packets sent our way
            if (data[0] == '$') {
                socket.write('+');
                if (data[1] == 'W') {
                    // The app process has exited, with hex status given by data[2-3] 
                    var status = parseInt(data.substring(2, 4), 16)
                    socket.endStatus = status;
                    socket.end();
                } else if (data[1] == 'X') {
                    // The app rocess exited because of signal given by data[2-3]
                    var signal = parseInt(data.substring(2, 4), 16)
                    socket.endSignal = signal;
                    socket.end();
                } else if (data.substring(1, 3) == 'OK') {
                    // last command was received OK;
                    if (socket.initState == 1) {
                        deferred1.resolve(socket);
                    } else if (socket.initState == 2) {
                        deferred2.resolve(socket);
                    }
                } else if (data[1] == 'O') {
                    // STDOUT was written to, and the rest of the input until reaching a '#' is a hex-encoded string of that output
                    if (socket.initState == 3) {
                        console.info("App started!");
                        deferred3.resolve(socket);
                        socket.initState++;
                    }
                } else if (data[1] == 'E') {
                    // An error has occurred, with error code given by data[2-3]
                    deferred1.reject("Launch failed: " + parseInt(data.substring(2, 4), 16));
                    deferred2.reject("Launch failed: " + parseInt(data.substring(2, 4), 16));
                    deferred3.reject("Launch failed: " + parseInt(data.substring(2, 4), 16));
                }
                
            }
        });
        
        socket.on("end", function () {
            deferred1.reject("Unable to launch app");
            deferred2.reject("Unable to launch app");
            deferred3.reject("Unable to launch app");
        });
 
        socket.connect(portNumber, "localhost", function () {
            // set argument 0 to the (encoded) path of the app
            console.info("Starting app...");
            var cmd = makeGdbCommand("A" + encodedPath.length + ",0," + encodedPath);
            socket.initState++;
            socket.write(cmd);
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (socket.initState == 1) {
                    deferred1.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    deferred2.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    deferred3.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    socket.end();
                }
            }, 5000);
        });
        
        return deferred1.promise.then(function (sock) {
            // Set the step and continue thread to any thread
            var cmd = makeGdbCommand("Hc0");
            sock.initState++;
            sock.write(cmd);
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (socket.initState == 2) {
                    deferred2.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    deferred3.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    socket.end();
                }
            }, 5000);
            return deferred2.promise;
        }).then(function (sock) {
            //Continue execution; actually start the app running.
            var cmd = makeGdbCommand("c");
            sock.initState++;
            sock.write(cmd);
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (socket.initState == 3) {
                    deferred3.reject("Timeout: Is the device locked?");
                    socket.end();
                }
            }, 5000);
            return deferred3.promise;
        });
    }
}
 
// Attempt to start the app on the device, using the debug server proxy on a given port.
// Returns a socket speaking remote gdb protocol with the debug server proxy.
runner.startApp = function (packageId, portNumber) {
    // When a user has many apps installedl on their device, the response from ideviceinstaller may be large (500k or more)
    // This exceeds the maximum stdout size that exec allows, so we redirect to a temp file.
    return promiseExec('ideviceinstaller -l -o xml > /tmp/$$.ideviceinstaller && echo /tmp/$$.ideviceinstaller').then(function (args) {
        // First find the path of the app on the device
        var filename = args[0].trim();
        if (! /^\/tmp\/[0-9]+\.ideviceinstaller$/.test(filename)) {
            throw new Error("Output file not as expected");
        }
        var list = pl.parseFileSync(filename);
        fs.unlink(filename);
        for (var i = 0; i < list.length; ++i) {
            if (list[i].CFBundleIdentifier == packageId) {
                return list[i].Path;
            }
        }
        throw new Error("Package not installed?");
    }).then(runner.startAppViaDebugger(portNumber));
}
 
function charToHex(char) {
    var conversionTable = '0123456789ABCDEF';
    var charCode = char.charCodeAt(0);
    return conversionTable[(charCode & 0xF0) >> 4] + conversionTable[charCode & 0x0F];
}
 
function makeGdbCommand(command) {
    var commandString = "$" + command + "#";
    var stringSum = 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < command.length; i++) {
        stringSum += command.charCodeAt(i);
    }
    stringSum = stringSum & 0xFF;
    var checksum = stringSum.toString(16).toUpperCase();
    if (checksum.length < 2) {
        checksum = '0' + checksum;
    }
    commandString += checksum;
    return commandString;
}

    baseBuildDir,

var mgr = exports = module.exports = {};
 
mgr.init = function (conf) {
    serverDir = conf.get('serverDir'),
    baseBuildDir = path.resolve(process.cwd(), serverDir, 'builds');
    util.createDirectoryIfNecessary(baseBuildDir);
    maxBuildsInQueue = conf.get('maxBuildsInQueue');
    deleteBuildsOnShutdown = util.argToBool(conf.get('deleteBuildsOnShutdown'));
    allowsEmulate = util.argToBool(conf.get('allowsEmulate'));
    nativeDebugProxyPort = conf.get('nativeDebugProxyPort');
    webDebugProxyDevicePort = conf.get('webDebugProxyDevicePort');
    webDebugProxyPortMin = conf.get('webDebugProxyRangeMin');
    webDebugProxyPortMax = conf.get('webDebugProxyRangeMax');
    if (allowsEmulate === true) {
        require('./emulate').init();
    }
    buildRetention.init(baseBuildDir, conf);
    // For now, using process startup pid as the initial build number is good enough to avoid collisions with prior server runs against 
    // the same base build dir, especially when build cleanup is used.
    nextBuildNumber = process.pid;
    builds = {};
    buildMetrics = {
        submitted: 0,
        accepted: 0,
        rejected: 0,
        failed: 0,
        succeeded: 0,
        downloaded: 0
    };
    currentBuild = null;
    queuedBuilds = [];
    console.info('Initialized BuildManager with baseBuildDir %s; maxBuildsInQueue %d; ' +
                 'deleteBuildsOnShutdown %s; allowsEmulate %s; nextBuildNumber %d',
                 baseBuildDir, maxBuildsInQueue, deleteBuildsOnShutdown, allowsEmulate, nextBuildNumber);
};
 
mgr.shutdown = function () {
    if (deleteBuildsOnShutdown === true) {
        buildRetention.deleteAllSync(builds);
    }
    runner.shutdown();
};
 
// Submit new build from the http request, calls the callback when the build has been validated and queued up
mgr.submitNewBuild = function (req, callback) {
    console.info('New build request submitted:');
    console.info(req.url);
    console.info(req.headers);
 
    buildMetrics.submitted++;
 
    if (queuedBuilds.length === maxBuildsInQueue) {
        // Ideally we would return a Http 503 Service Unavailable
        callback('Build request rejected. The build queue is full. Limit is ' + maxBuildsInQueue + ' queued builds.');
        return;
    }
 
    // For now these are part of the request query (after the ?) but might look to make these part of the path, or headers, as most are not really optional parameters
    var cordovaVersion = req.query.vcordova || null;
    var buildCommand = req.query.command || 'build';
    var configuration = req.query.cfg || 'release';
    var options = req.query.options || '';
    var buildNumber = req.query.buildNumber || null;
 
    console.info('New build request submitted for cordovaVersion: ' + cordovaVersion + '; buildCommand: ' + buildCommand + '; configuration: ' + configuration);
    var requestErrors = validateBuildRequest(req.headers['accept-language'], cordovaVersion, buildCommand, configuration);
    if (requestErrors.length > 0) {
        callback(requestErrors);
        buildMetrics.rejected++;
        return;
    }
    buildMetrics.accepted++;
 
    if (!buildNumber) {
        buildNumber = ++nextBuildNumber;
    }
    var buildDir = path.join(baseBuildDir, '' + buildNumber);
    if (!fs.existsSync(buildDir)) {
        fs.mkdirSync(buildDir);
    }
    console.info('Build will be executed under: ' + buildDir);
 
    var buildInfo = new bi.BuildInfo(buildNumber, bi.UPLOADING, cordovaVersion, buildCommand, configuration, options, buildDir, serverDir);
    builds[buildNumber] = buildInfo;
 
    saveUploadedTgzFile(buildInfo, req, function (err, result) {
        if (err) {
            callback(err);
        } else {
            callback(null, buildInfo);
            beginBuild(buildInfo);
        }
    });
};
 
// Downloads the requested build.
mgr.downloadBuild = function (id, res, callback) {
    console.info('Transferring result of build ' + id + ' ...');
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        var msg = 'Unknown build ' + id + ' in transfer request';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
    else if (buildInfo.status !== bi.COMPLETE && buildInfo.status !== bi.DOWNLOADED) {
        var msg = 'Requested build is not available for transfer. Status: ' + buildInfo.status;
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg, buildInfo);
        return;
    }
    var platformOutputDir = path.join(buildInfo.appDir, 'platforms', 'ios', 'build', 'device');
    var pathToPlistFile = path.join(platformOutputDir, buildInfo.appName + '.plist');
    var pathToIpaFile = path.join(platformOutputDir, buildInfo.appName + '.ipa');
    if (!fs.existsSync(pathToPlistFile) || !fs.existsSync(pathToIpaFile)) {
        var msg = 'One or both of expected build outputs ' + pathToPlistFile + ' and ' + pathToIpaFile + ' are missing on file system.';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg, buildInfo);
        return;
    }
 
    var archive = new packer();
    archive.on('error', function (err) {
        console.error('Error from archiving ' + err.message, err);
        callback(err, buildInfo);
    });
    res.set({ 'Content-Type': 'application/zip' });
    archive.pipe(res);
    archive.entry(fs.createReadStream(pathToPlistFile), { name: buildInfo.appName + '.plist' }, function (err, file) {
        if (err) {
            console.error('Error from archiving plist file ' + err.message, err);
            callback(err, buildInfo);
            return;
        }
        archive.entry(fs.createReadStream(pathToIpaFile), { name: buildInfo.appName + '.ipa' }, function (err, file) {
            if (err) {
                console.error('Error from archiving ipa file ' + err.message, err);
                callback(err, buildInfo);
                return;
            }
            archive.finalize();
            console.info('Trasnferred build ' + id);
            buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.DOWNLOADED);
            buildMetrics.downloaded++;
            callback(null, buildInfo);
        });
    });
};
 
mgr.getBuildInfo = function (id) {
    return builds[id] || null;
};
 
mgr.getDebugPort = function () {
    return webDebugProxyDevicePort;
}
 
mgr.getAllBuildInfo = function () {
    return {
        metrics: buildMetrics,
        queued: queuedBuilds.length,
        currentBuild: currentBuild,
        queuedBuilds: queuedBuilds,
        allBuilds: builds
    };
};
 
mgr.downloadBuildLog = function (id, res) {
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        res.end();
        return;
    }
    var buildLog = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'build.log');
    if (!fs.existsSync(buildLog)) {
        res.end();
        return;
    }
    var logStream = fs.createReadStream(buildLog);
    logStream.on('error', function (err) {
        console.info('Error from reading build log file ' + buildLog + ': ' + err);
    });
    logStream.pipe(res);
};
 
mgr.emulateBuild = function (id, target, callback) {
    if (allowsEmulate === false) {
        callback('Emulate is not enabled on this server.');
        return;
    }
    console.info('Emulate build %s %s ...', id, target);
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        var msg = 'Unknown build ' + id + ' in emulateBuild request';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
    var cfg = new CordovaConfig(path.join(buildInfo.appDir, 'config.xml'));
    var cordovaAppDir = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'cordovaApp');
    if (!fs.existsSync(cordovaAppDir)) {
        var msg = 'App does not exist in build directory ' + cordovaAppDir;
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
    console.info('Emulating app under ' + cordovaAppDir);
    var emulate = require('child_process').fork(path.join(__dirname, 'emulate.js'), [], { silent: true });
    var emulateLogger = new BuildLogger();
    emulateLogger.begin(buildInfo.buildDir, 'emulate.log', emulate);
    emulate.send({ appDir: cordovaAppDir, appName: cfg.id(), target: target });
    emulate.on('message', function (result) {
        console.info('Result from emulate child process: ' + result.status + '; ' + result.messageId + '; ' + result.messageArgs);
        buildInfo.updateStatus(result.status, result.messageId, result.messageArgs);
        callback(null, buildInfo);
        emulate.kill();
        emulateLogger.end();
        return;
    });
};
 
mgr.installBuild = function (id, callback) {
    console.info('Deploy build %s ...', id);
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        var msg = 'Unknown build ' + id + ' in deploy request';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
    var pathToIpaFile = path.join(buildInfo.appDir, 'platforms', 'ios', 'build', 'device', buildInfo.appName + '.ipa');
    installer.install(pathToIpaFile).then(function (success) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.INSTALLED, 'InstallSuccess');
        callback(null, buildInfo);
    }, function (error) {
        callback(error);
    })
}
 
mgr.runBuild = function (id, callback) {
    console.info('Run build %s ...', id);
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        var msg = 'Unknown build ' + id + ' in runBuild request';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
 
    var cfg = new CordovaConfig(path.join(buildInfo.appDir, 'config.xml'));
    var packageId = cfg.id()
 
    runner.startDebugProxy(nativeDebugProxyPort).then(function (success) {
        var proxy = success;
        return runner.startApp(packageId, nativeDebugProxyPort);
    }).then(function (success) {
        var socket = success;
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.RUNNING, 'RunSuccess');
        callback(null, buildInfo);
    }, function (failure) {
        console.info(failure);
        callback(failure);
    })
}
 
mgr.debugBuild = function (id, callback) {
    console.info('Debug build %s ...', id);
    var buildInfo = builds[id];
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        var msg = 'Unknown build ' + id + ' in runBuild request';
        console.info(msg);
        callback(msg);
        return;
    }
 
    runner.startiOSWebkitDebugProxy(webDebugProxyDevicePort, webDebugProxyPortMin, webDebugProxyPortMax).then(function (webkitDebugProxy) {
        buildInfo.webDebugProxyPort = webDebugProxyDevicePort;
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.DEBUGGING, 'DebugSuccess');
        callback(null, buildInfo);
    }, function (failure) {
        callback(failure);
    })
}
 
mgr.getBaseBuildDir = function () {
    return baseBuildDir;
};
 
function validateBuildRequest(acceptLangsHeader, cordovaVersion, buildCommand, configuration) {
    var errors = [];
    if (cordovaVersion === null) {
        errors.push(res.getString(acceptLangsHeader, 'BuildRequestMissingCordovaVersion'));
    }
    if (buildCommand !== 'build') {
        errors.push(res.getString(acceptLangsHeader, 'BuildRequestUnsupportedCommand', buildCommand));
    }
    if (configuration !== 'debug' && configuration !== 'release') {
        errors.push(res.getString(acceptLangsHeader, 'BuildRequestUnsupportedConfiguration', configuration));
    }
    return errors;
}
 
function saveUploadedTgzFile(buildInfo, req, callback) {
    console.info('Saving build request payload to : ' + buildInfo.buildDir);
    buildInfo.tgzFilePath = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'upload_' + buildInfo.buildNumber + '.tgz');
    var tgzFile = fs.createWriteStream(buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
    req.pipe(tgzFile);
    tgzFile.on('finish', function () {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.UPLOADED);
        console.info('Saved upload to ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
        callback(null, buildInfo);
    });
    tgzFile.on('error', function (err) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, 'An error occurred in saving the uploaded tgz file to ' + tgzFile + ': ' + err.message);
        console.error('Could not save the uploaded tgz file to ' + tgzFile + ' : ' + err);
        buildMetrics.failed++;
        callback(err, buildInfo);
    });
}
 
function beginBuild(buildInfo) {
    var extractToDir = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'cordovaApp');
    try {
        if (!fs.existsSync(extractToDir)) {
            fs.mkdirSync(extractToDir);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, 'Unable to create extract directory ' + extractToDir + ': ' + e.message);
        console.error('Build tgz file no longer exists on file system at ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
        buildMetrics.failed++;
        return;
    }
 
    console.info('Extracting ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath + ' to ' + extractToDir + '...');
    if (!fs.existsSync(buildInfo.tgzFilePath)) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, 'The tgz file for the build no longer exists on file system: ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
        console.error('Build tgz file no longer exists on file system at ' + buiildInfo.tgzFilePath);
        buildMetrics.failed++;
        return;
    }
    var onError = function (err) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, 'An error occurred in extracting contents from ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath + ': ' + err.message);
        console.info('An error occurred in extracting contents from ' + buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
        buildMetrics.failed++;
    };
 
    // A tar file created on windows has no notion of 'rwx' attributes on a directory, so directories are not executable when 
    // extracting to unix, causing the extract to fail because the directory cannot be navigated. 
    // Also, the tar module does not handle an 'error' event from it's underlying stream, so we have no way of catching errors like an unwritable
    // directory in the tar gracefully- they cause an uncaughtException and server shutdown. For safety sake we force 'rwx' for all on everything.
    var tarFilter = function (who) {
        if (path.basename(who.props.path) === 'config.json' && path.basename(path.dirname(who.props.path)) === '.cordova') {
            console.info('Not extracting .cordova/config.json. It is used on individual developer machines to customize locations of libraries ' +
                        'and will not work on a remote machine.');
            return false;
        }
        who.props.mode = 511; // "chmod 777"
        return true;
    }
 
    // strip: 1 means take the top level directory name off when extracting (we want 'cordovaApp' to be the top level dir.)
    var tarExtractor = tar.Extract({ path: extractToDir, strip: 1, filter: tarFilter });
    tarExtractor.on('end', function () {
        removeDeletedFiles(buildInfo);
 
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.EXTRACTED);
        console.info('Extracted app contents from uploaded build request to %s. Requesting build.', extractToDir);
        build(buildInfo);
    });
    var unzip = zlib.createGunzip();
    var tgzStream = fs.createReadStream(buildInfo.tgzFilePath);
    tarExtractor.on('error', onError);
    unzip.on('error', onError);
    tgzStream.on('error', onError).pipe(unzip).on('error', onError).pipe(tarExtractor).on('error', onError);
}
 
function removeDeletedFiles(buildInfo) {
    var cordovaDir = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'cordovaApp');
    var changeListFile = path.join(cordovaDir, 'changeList.json');
    if (fs.existsSync(changeListFile)) {
        buildInfo.changeList = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(changeListFile, { encoding: 'utf-8' }));
        if (buildInfo.changeList) {
            buildInfo.changeList.deletedFiles.forEach(function (deletedFile) {
                var fileToDelete = path.join(cordovaDir, path.normalize(deletedFile));
                if (fs.existsSync(fileToDelete)) {
                    fs.unlinkSync(fileToDelete);
                }
            });
        }
    }
}
 
// Cordova build relies on changing current working directory to the cordova app dir. To build multiple builds in parallel we will
// need to fork out child processes. For now, limiting to one build at a time, and queuing up new builds that come in while a current build is in progress.
function build(buildInfo) {
    if (currentBuild !== null) {
        console.info('A build is currently building. Queuing up ' + buildInfo.buildNumber);
        queuedBuilds.push(buildInfo);
        return;
    } else {
        console.info('Taking ' + buildInfo.buildNumber + ' as current build');
        currentBuild = buildInfo;
    }
 
    // Good point to purge old builds
    buildRetention.purge(builds);
 
    buildInfo.appDir = path.join(buildInfo.buildDir, 'cordovaApp');
    if (!fs.existsSync(buildInfo.appDir)) {
        var msg = 'Build directory ' + buildInfo.buildDir + ' does not exist.';
        console.info(msg);
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, msg);
        buildMetrics.failed++;
        dequeueNextBuild();
        return;
    }
 
    var cordovaAppError = validateCordovaApp(buildInfo.appDir);
    if (cordovaAppError !== null) {
        buildMetrics.rejected++;
        buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.INVALID, cordovaAppError.id, cordovaAppError.args);
        console.info('Not building buildNumber [' + buildInfo.buildNumber + '] because it is not a valid Cordova Application: ' + cordovaAppError);
        dequeueNextBuild();
        return;
    }
 
    var cfg = new CordovaConfig(path.join(buildInfo.appDir, 'config.xml'));
    buildInfo.appName = cfg.name();
 
    console.info('Building cordova app %s at appDir %s', buildInfo.appName, buildInfo.appDir);
    buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.BUILDING);
 
    // Fork off to a child build process. This allows us to save off all stdout for that build to it's own log file. And in future we can 
    // have multiple builds in parallel by forking multiple child processes (with some max limit.)
    var buildProcess = require('child_process').fork(path.join(__dirname, 'build.js'), [], { silent: true });
    var buildLogger = new BuildLogger();
    buildLogger.begin(buildInfo.buildDir, 'build.log', buildProcess);
    buildProcess.send(buildInfo);
    buildProcess.on('message', function (resultBuildInfo) {
        buildInfo.updateStatus(resultBuildInfo.status, resultBuildInfo.messageId, resultBuildInfo.messageArgs);
        console.info('Done building %d : %s %s', buildInfo.buildNumber, buildInfo.status, buildInfo.messageId, buildInfo.messageArgs);
        if (buildInfo.status === bi.COMPLETE) {
            buildMetrics.succeeded++;
        } else {
            buildMetrics.failed++;
        }
        buildProcess.kill();
        buildLogger.end();
        dequeueNextBuild();
    });
    buildProcess.on('exit', function (exitCode) {
        if (buildInfo.status === bi.BUILDING) {
            buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.ERROR, 'BuildFailedWithError', 'Build process unexpectedly exited');
            buildMetrics.failed++;
            buildLogger.end();
            dequeueNextBuild();
        }
    });
}
 
function dequeueNextBuild() {
    console.info('Done with currentBuild. Checking for next build in queue.');
    currentBuild = null;
    var nextBuild = queuedBuilds.shift();
    if (nextBuild) {
        console.info('Dequeued ' + nextBuild.buildNumber + ' and will build that next');
        build(nextBuild);
    }
}
 
// This is basic validation. The build itself will fail if config.xml is not valid, or more detailed problems with the submission.
function validateCordovaApp(appDir) {
    if (!fs.existsSync(path.join(appDir, 'config.xml'))) {
        return { id: 'InvalidCordovaAppMissingConfigXml' };
    } else {
        try {
            var cfg = new CordovaConfig(path.join(currentBuild.appDir, 'config.xml'));
            var appName = cfg.name();
            if (!util.isValidCordovaAppName(appName)) {
                return { id: 'InvalidCordovaAppUnsupportedAppName', args: [appName, util.invalidAppNameCharacters()] };
                errors.push('Invalid iOS app name ' + appName + ' in config.xml. Check for characters that are not Printable ASCII, or that match any of the following characters: ' +
                                util.invalidAppNameCharacters());
            }
            // TODO validate that start page exists (content src='index.html')
        } catch (e) {
            return { id: 'InvalidCordovaAppBadConfigXml', args: e.message };
        }
    }
 
    if (!fs.existsSync(path.join(appDir, 'www'))) {
        return { id: 'InvalidCordovaAppMissingWww' };
    }
 
    return null;
}
 
function deleteBuild(buildInfo) {
    buildRetention.deleteBuildDirectory(buildInfo.buildDir, function (err) {
        if (err) {
            console.error('Failed to delete build directory: ' + buildInfo.buildDir);
        } else {
            buildInfo.updateStatus(bi.DELETED);
            console.info('Deleted build directory: ' + buildInfo.buildDir);
        }
    });
}

/********************************************************

"use strict";
 
var bi = require('./BuildInfo'),
    rimraf = require('rimraf');
 
var br = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var baseBuildDir;
var maxBuildsToKeep;
 
br.init = function(baseBuildDir, conf) {
    maxBuildsToKeep = conf.get('maxBuildsToKeep');
    console.info('Build Retention initialized with baseBuildDir %s, maxBuildsToKeep %d', baseBuildDir, maxBuildsToKeep);
};
 
br.purge = function(builds) {
    var buildNumbers = Object.keys(builds);
    var nBuildsToDelete = buildNumbers.length - maxBuildsToKeep;
    if (nBuildsToDelete <= 0) {
        return;
    }
 
    // eligible builds do not include those queued up or currently building.
    var eligibleBuilds = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < buildNumbers.length; i++) {
        var buildInfo = builds[buildNumbers[i]];
        if (buildInfo.status === bi.COMPLETE || buildInfo.status === bi.DOWNLOADED ||
            buildInfo.status === bi.DELETED || buildInfo.status === bi.ERROR ||
            buildInfo.status === bi.EMULATED || buildInfo.status === bi.INVALID) {
            eligibleBuilds.push(buildInfo);
        }
    };
    // sort eligible builds by oldest first, then delete required number
    eligibleBuilds.sort(function(b1, b2) {
        var diff = b1.submissionTime - b2.submissionTime;
        return (diff === 0) ? 0 : (diff > 0 ? +1 : -1);
    });
    if (nBuildsToDelete > eligibleBuilds.length) {
        nBuildsToDelete = eligibleBuilds.length;
    }
    console.info('Deleting eligible builds. Will delete %d builds.', nBuildsToDelete);
    for (var i = 0; i < nBuildsToDelete; i++) {
        var buildInfo = eligibleBuilds[i];
        console.info('Deleting build %d from %s', buildInfo.buildNumber, buildInfo.buildDir);
        br.deleteBuildDirectory(buildInfo.buildDir);
        delete builds[eligibleBuilds[i].buildNumber];
    }
};
 
br.deleteAllSync = function(builds) {
    var buildNumbers = Object.keys(builds);
    for (var i = 0; i < buildNumbers.length; i++) {
        var buildInfo = builds[buildNumbers[i]];
        console.info('Deleting build %d from %s', buildInfo.buildNumber, buildInfo.buildDir);
        rimraf.sync(buildInfo.buildDir);
        delete builds[buildNumbers[i]];
    }
};
 
br.deleteBuildDirectory = function(buildDir, callback) {
    rimraf(buildDir, function(err) {
        if (callback) {
            callback(err);
        }
    });
};

"use strict";
 
var exec = require("child_process").exec,
    path = require('path'),
    fs = require('fs'),
    os = require('os'),
    readline = require('readline'),
    Q = require('q'),
    rimraf = require('rimraf'),
    util = require('./util');
 
var certs = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var CERT_DEFAULTS = {
    DAYS: 1825, // 5 years
    COUNTRY: 'US',
    CA_CN: 'vs-mda-remote-Certificate-Authority',
    PFX_NAME: 'vs-mda-remote-Client-Certificate'
};
 
var ONE_DAY_IN_MILLIS = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;
 
certs.initializeServerCerts = function(conf) {
    var certsDir = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs');
    var certPaths = {
        certsDir: certsDir,
        caKeyPath: path.join(certsDir, 'ca-key.pem'),
        caCertPath: path.join(certsDir, 'ca-cert.pem'),
        serverKeyPath: path.join(certsDir, 'server-key.pem'),
        serverCertPath: path.join(certsDir, 'server-cert.pem')
    };
 
    var certsExist = fs.existsSync(certPaths.caCertPath) && fs.existsSync(certPaths.serverKeyPath) && fs.existsSync(certPaths.serverCertPath);
    certPaths.newCerts = !certsExist;
    var promise;
    if (certsExist) {
        promise = certs.isExpired(certPaths.caCertPath).
                    then(function(isExpired) {
                        return isExpired === true || certs.isExpired(certPaths.serverCertPath);
                    });
    } else {
        promise = Q(true); // do not exist, so true -> need making
    }
 
    promise = promise.then(function(shouldMake) {
        if (shouldMake === false) {
            return;
        }
        util.createDirectoryIfNecessary(certsDir);
        var options = certOptionsFromConf(conf);
        return certs.makeSelfSigningCACert(certPaths.caKeyPath, certPaths.caCertPath, options).
            then(function() {
                return certs.makeSelfSignedCert(certPaths.caKeyPath, certPaths.caCertPath, certPaths.serverKeyPath, certPaths.serverCertPath, options, conf);
            }).
            then(function() {
                certPaths.newCerts = true;
            });
    }).then(function() {
        return certPaths;
    });
    return promise;
}
 
// yesOrNoHandler is for unit testing without interactive user prompt. In production it will be undefined.
certs.resetServerCert = function(conf, yesOrNoHandler) {
    var certsDir = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs');
 
    if (!fs.existsSync(certsDir)) {
        return certs.initializeServerCerts(conf);
    }
 
    var shouldProceedDeferred = Q.defer();
    yesOrNoHandler = yesOrNoHandler || readline.createInterface({input: process.stdin, output: process.stdout});
    var answerCallback = function(answer) {
        answer = answer.toLowerCase();
        if (answer === 'y' || answer === 'yes') {
            yesOrNoHandler.close();
            shouldProceedDeferred.resolve(true);
        } else if (answer === 'n' || answer === 'no') {
            yesOrNoHandler.close();
            shouldProceedDeferred.resolve(false);
        } else {
            yesOrNoHandler.question('Please answer [Y]es or [N]o.' + os.EOL, answerCallback);
        }
    };
    yesOrNoHandler.question('Warning: This command deletes all current client certificates. ' +
                        'You will need to generate and configure a new security PIN. Do you want to continue? [Y]es or [N]o' + os.EOL, answerCallback);
    return shouldProceedDeferred.promise.
            then(function(shouldProceed) {
                if (shouldProceed == true) {
                    rimraf.sync(certsDir);
                    return certs.initializeServerCerts(conf);
                }
            });
};
 
certs.generateClientCert = function(conf) {
    var certsDir = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs');
    var caKeyPath = path.join(certsDir, 'ca-key.pem');
    var caCertPath = path.join(certsDir, 'ca-cert.pem');
    if (!fs.existsSync(caKeyPath) || !fs.existsSync(caCertPath)) {
        return Q(console.info('One or both of required CA files %s and %s not found.', caKeyPath, caCertPath));
    }
    return makeClientPinAndSslCert(caKeyPath, caCertPath, certsDir, certOptionsFromConf(conf), conf).
            then(function(pin) {
                if (util.argToBool(conf.get('suppressVisualStudioMessage'))) {
                    return pin;
                }
                certs.printVisualStudioSetupToConsole(conf, pin);
                return pin;
            });
};
 
certs.printVisualStudioSetupToConsole = function(conf, pin) {
    var host = conf.hostname || os.hostname();
    var port = conf.get('port');
    var pinTimeoutInMinutes = conf.get('pinTimeout');
    console.info('');
    console.info('First Time Setup');
    console.info('---------------------');
    console.info('Use the following information under Tools, Options, Tools for Apache Cordova, Remote Agent Configuration to configure this agent:');
    console.info('');
    console.info('Enable remote iOS processing: True');
    console.info('Host: %s', host || '<IP address of your Mac>');
    console.info('Port: %s', port || '3000 <or specific port you have configured for the agent to use>');
    console.info('Secure mode: True');
    console.info('Security PIN: %d', pin);
    console.info('');
    if (pinTimeoutInMinutes) {
        console.info('The security PIN is for one-time use and expires in %d minutes. To generate additional PINs, use the following command:', pinTimeoutInMinutes);
    } else {
        console.info('The security PIN is for one-time use. To generate additional PINs, use the following command:');
    }
    console.info('vs-mda-remote generateClientCert');
    console.info('');
};
 
certs.removeAllCertsSync = function(conf) {
    var certsDir = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs');
    if (fs.existsSync(certsDir)) {
        rimraf.sync(certsDir);
    }
};
 
certs.purgeExpiredPinBasedClientCertsSync = function(conf) {
    var clientCertsDir = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs', 'client');
    if (!fs.existsSync(clientCertsDir)) {
        return;
    }
    var pinTimeoutInMinutes = conf.get('pinTimeout');
    var expiredIfOlderThan = new Date().getTime() - (pinTimeoutInMinutes * 60 * 1000);
    fs.readdirSync(clientCertsDir).forEach(function(f) {
        var pfx = path.join(clientCertsDir, f, 'client.pfx');
        if (fs.existsSync(pfx) && fs.statSync(pfx).mtime.getTime() < expiredIfOlderThan) {
            rimraf.sync(path.join(clientCertsDir, f));
        }
    });
};
 
// Makes a CA cert that will be used for self-signing our server and client certs.
certs.makeSelfSigningCACert = function(caKeyPath, caCertPath, options) {
    options = options || {};
    var days = options.days || CERT_DEFAULTS.DAYS;
    var country = options.country || CERT_DEFAULTS.COUNTRY;
    var cn = options.cn || CERT_DEFAULTS.CA_CN;
    return openSslPromise('req -newkey rsa:4096 -x509 -days ' + days + ' -nodes -subj /C=' + country + '/CN=' + cn + ' -keyout ' + caKeyPath + ' -out ' + caCertPath);
};
 
// Makes a new private key and certificate signed with the CA.
certs.makeSelfSignedCert = function(caKeyPath, caCertPath, outKeyPath, outCertPath, options, conf) {
    options = options || {};
    var csrPath = path.join(path.dirname(outCertPath), 'CSR-' + path.basename(outCertPath));
    var days = options.days || CERT_DEFAULTS.DAYS;;
    var cn = options.cn || os.hostname();
    
    var cnfPath = path.join(conf.get('serverDir'), 'certs', 'openssl.cnf');
    certs.writeConfigFile(cnfPath);
 
    return openSslPromise('genrsa -out ' + outKeyPath + ' 1024').
        then(function() {
            return openSslPromise('req -new -subj /CN=' + cn + ' -key ' + outKeyPath + ' -out ' + csrPath + ' -config ' + cnfPath);
        }).
        then(function() {
            return openSslPromise('x509 -req -days ' + days + ' -in ' + csrPath + ' -CA ' + caCertPath + ' -CAkey ' + caKeyPath + 
                                    ' -extensions v3_req -extfile ' + cnfPath + ' -set_serial 01 -out ' + outCertPath);
        }).
        then(function() {
            fs.unlinkSync(csrPath);
        });
};
 
certs.writeConfigFile = function(cnfPath) {
    var net = os.networkInterfaces();
    var cnf = '[req]\ndistinguished_name = req_distinguished_name\nreq_extensions = v3_req\n[req_distinguished_name]\nC_default = US\n[ v3_req ]\nbasicConstraints = CA:FALSE\nkeyUsage = nonRepudiation, digitalSignature, keyEncipherment\nsubjectAltName = @alt_names\n[alt_names]\nDNS.1 = ' + os.hostname() + '\n';
    var count = 1;
 
    for (var key in net) {
        for (var i = 0; i < net[key].length; i++) {
            if (net[key][i].address && !net[key][i].internal) {
                cnf += 'IP.' + count + ' = ' + net[key][i].address + '\n';
                count++;
            }
        }
    }
 
    fs.writeFileSync(cnfPath, cnf);
}
 
certs.makePfx = function(caCertPath, keyPath, certPath, outPfxPath, options) {
    options = options || {};
    var name = options.name || CERT_DEFAULTS.PFX_NAME;
    return openSslPromise('pkcs12 -export -in ' + certPath + ' -inkey ' + keyPath + ' -certfile ' + caCertPath + ' -out ' + outPfxPath + 
                            ' -name \'' + name + '\' -password pass:');
}
 
certs.verifyCert = function(caCertPath, certPath) {
    return openSslPromise('verify -CAfile ' + caCertPath + ' ' + certPath);
};
 
// display fields an array of any of these: 'subject', 'issuer', 'dates', etc. (see https://www.openssl.org/docs/apps/x509.html)
certs.displayCert = function(certPath, displayFields) {
    //openssl x509 -noout -in selfsigned-cert.pem -subject -issuer -dates
    var args = 'x509 -noout -in ' + certPath;
    (displayFields || []).forEach(function(f) {
        args += ' -' + f;
    });
    return openSslPromise(args);
};
 
certs.isExpired = function(certPath) {
    return certs.displayCert(certPath, ['dates']).
            then(function(output) {
                var notAfter = new Date(output.stdout.substring(output.stdout.indexOf('notAfter=')+9, output.stdout.length-1));
                return (notAfter.getTime() < new Date().getTime());
            });
};
 
certs.verbose = false;
 
function makeClientPinAndSslCert(caKeyPath, caCertPath, certsDir, options, conf) {
    options = options || {};
    options.cn = 'vs-mda-remote-client';
    var clientCertsPath = path.join(certsDir, 'client');
    util.createDirectoryIfNecessary(clientCertsPath);
    // 6 digit random pin (Math.random excludes 1.0)
    var pin = 100000 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 900000);
    var pinDir = path.join(clientCertsPath, '' + pin);
    var pfxPath = path.join(pinDir, 'client.pfx');
    var clientKeyPath = path.join(pinDir, 'client-key.pem');
    var clientCertPath = path.join(pinDir, 'client-cert.pem');
 
    util.createDirectoryIfNecessary(pinDir);
    return certs.makeSelfSignedCert(caKeyPath, caCertPath, clientKeyPath, clientCertPath, options, conf).
            then(function() {
                return certs.makePfx(caCertPath, clientKeyPath, clientCertPath, pfxPath);
            }).
            then(function() {
                fs.unlinkSync(clientKeyPath);
                fs.unlinkSync(clientCertPath);
                return pin;
            });
}
 
function certOptionsFromConf(conf) {
    var options = {};
    if (conf.get('certExpirationDays') < 1) {
        console.info('certExpirationDays %d would result in expired certs. Default cert expiration %d days will be used instead.', conf.get('certExpirationDays'), CERT_DEFAULTS.DAYS);
    } else {
        options.days = conf.get('certExpirationDays');
    }
    return options;
}
 
function openSslPromise(args) {
    var deferred = Q.defer();
 
    exec('openssl ' + args, function(error, stdout, stderr) {
        if (certs.verbose) {
            console.info('exec openssl ' + args);
            console.info('stdout: %s', stdout);
            console.info('stderr: %s', stderr);
        }
        if (error !== null) {
            deferred.reject(error);
        } else {
            deferred.resolve({stdout: stdout, stderr: stderr});
        }
    });
 
    return deferred.promise;
}

/********************************************************
*                                                       *
*   Copyright (C) Microsoft. All rights reserved.       *
*                                                       *
********************************************************/
"use strict";
 
var path = require('path'),
    nconf = require('nconf'),
    server = require('./server'),
    fs = require("fs"),
    readlineSync = require("readline-sync"),
    child_process = require('child_process'),
    Q = require("q"),
    resources = require("./resources");
 
module.exports = function() {
 
    console.info('vs-mda-remote');
    console.info('Copyright (C) 2014 Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.');
    console.info(require('../package').version);
    console.info('');
 
    // Configuration preference: command line, then anything in a config file if specified by the --config arg, then some defaults for options not yet set
    nconf.argv();
    if (nconf.get('v') || nconf.get('version')) {
        process.exit(0);
    }
    if (nconf.get('config')) {
        nconf.file({ file: nconf.get('config') });
    };
    nconf.defaults({
        'serverDir': path.join(process.env.HOME, 'remote-builds'),
        'port': 3000,
        'maxBuildsInQueue': 10,
        'maxBuildsToKeep': 20,
        'deleteBuildsOnShutdown': true,
        'allowsEmulate': true,
        'secure': true,
        'pinTimeout': 10,
        'nativeDebugProxyPort': 3001,
        'webDebugProxyDevicePort': 9221,
        'webDebugProxyRangeMin': 9222,
        'webDebugProxyRangeMax': 9322,
        'writePidToFile': false,
        'lang': process.env.LANG &&  process.env.LANG.replace(/_.*/,"") || "en", // Convert "en_US.UTF8" to "en", similarly for other locales
    });
    // Initialize localization resources
    resources.init();
 
    if (nconf.get('help') || nconf.get('h') || nconf.get('?') || !nconf.get('serverDir')) {
        printUsage(nconf);
        process.exit(0);
    }
 
    var commands = nconf.get('_');
    var cmd = commands && commands.length > 0 ? commands[0] : 'start';
    if (cmd === 'resetServerCert') {
        server.resetServerCert(nconf);
    } else if (cmd === 'generateClientCert') {
        nconf.set('port', '3000 <or specific port youve configured for the agent to use>');
        nconf.set('pinTimeout', undefined);
        server.generateClientCert(nconf);
    } else if (cmd == 'start') {
        // Check first-run/third party installation
        var firstRunPath = path.join(process.env.HOME, ".vs-mda-remote")
        var isFirstRun = !fs.existsSync(firstRunPath);
        var deferred = Q.defer();
        if (isFirstRun) {
            console.info(resources.getString(nconf.get("lang"), "FirstRunDependencyConfiguration"));
            var response = readlineSync.question(resources.getString(nconf.get("lang"), "HomebrewInstallationQuery"));
            var shouldInstall = response === "" || response.toLowerCase().indexOf(resources.getString(nconf.get("lang"), "HomebrewInstallationQueryResponse")) === 0;
            var deferred2 = Q.defer();
 
            if (shouldInstall) {
                var homebrewInstalled = Q.defer();
                // We use spawn here rather than exec primarily so we can allow for user-interaction
                var curlInstaller = child_process.spawn('curl', ['-fsSL', 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Homebrew/install/master/install']);
                var installHomebrew = child_process.spawn('ruby', ['-']);
                
                curlInstaller.stdout.on('data', function (data) {
                    installHomebrew.stdin.write(data);
                });
                curlInstaller.on('close', function (code) {
                    installHomebrew.stdin.end();
                });
 
                installHomebrew.stdout.on('data', function (data) {
                    console.info("" + data);
                });
                installHomebrew.stderr.on('data', function (data) {
                    console.error("" + data);
                });
                installHomebrew.on('close', function (code) {
                    homebrewInstalled.resolve();
                });
                installHomebrew.on('error', function (arg) {
                    console.error("ERROR: " + JSON.stringify(arg));
                    process.exit(1);
                });
 
                homebrewInstalled.promise.then(function () {
                    // Install these packages if they do not exist.
                    // We need to check first since the install will fail if an older version is already installed.
                    // ideviceinstaller and ios-webkit-debug-proxy will install libimobiledevice if required
                    return Q.denodeify(child_process.exec)("(brew list ideviceinstaller | grep ideviceinstaller > /dev/null || brew install ideviceinstaller) && \
                                                            (brew list ios-webkit-debug-proxy | grep ios-webkit-debug-proxy > /dev/null || brew install ios-webkit-debug-proxy)");
                }).then(function (success) {
                    // Verify that both of these can run.
                    Q.denodeify(child_process.exec)("ideviceinstaller -h > /dev/null && ios_webkit_debug_proxy -h > /dev/null")
                    .then(function (success) {
                        console.info(resources.getString(nconf.get('lang'), "HomebrewInstallationSuccess"));
                        deferred2.resolve()
                    }, function (error) {
                        console.error(resources.getString(nconf.get('lang'), "HomebrewPackageVerificationFailed", error));
                        process.exit(1);
                    });
                }, function (error) {
                    console.error(resources.getString(nconf.get('lang'), "HomebrewInstallationFailed", error));
                    process.exit(1);
                });
            } else {
                console.info(resources.getString(nconf.get('lang'), "HomebrewInstallationDeclined"));
                deferred2.resolve();
            }
            
            deferred2.promise.then(function () {
                // Write to the file. We don't read the contents, but it may help with user discoverability if they change their mind
                fs.writeFileSync(firstRunPath, "installHomebrew = " + (shouldInstall? "yes" : "no") + "\n");
                deferred.resolve();
            })
        } else {
            deferred.resolve();
        }
 
        deferred.promise.then(function () {
            server.start(nconf);
        });
    } else {
        console.info(resources.getString(nconf.get('lang'), 'UnknownCommand'), cmd);
        printUsage(nconf);
        process.exit(0);
    }
};
 
function printUsage(conf) {
    console.info(resources.getString(conf.get('lang'), "UsageInformation").join('\n'));
}

"use strict";
 
var path = require('path'),
    fs = require('fs'),
    exec = require('child_process').exec,
    Q = require('q'),
    util = require('./util');
 
var e = exports = module.exports = {};
 
// will run as a forked child process because we do not want to change cwd on main process, where cordova relies on cwd being the app it is currently building
process.on('message', function (emulateRequest) {
    e.emulate(emulateRequest, function (result) {
        process.send(result);
    });
});
 
e.emulate = function(emulateRequest, callback) {
    console.info('Emulating app at ' + emulateRequest.appDir + ' for target ' + emulateRequest.target);
    var error = null;
 
    try {
        Q(cdToAppDir(emulateRequest)).
        then(cordovaEmulate).
        fail(function (err) {
            error = err;
        }).
        done(function () {
            if (error !== null) {
                callback({status: 'error', messageId: 'EmulateFailedWithError', messageArgs: error.message});
            } else {
                callback({status: 'emulated', messageId: 'EmulateSuccess'});
            }
        });
    } catch (e) {
        callback({status: 'error', messageId: 'EmulateFailedWithError', messageArgs: e.message});
    }
};
 
e.init = function() {
    process.env['PATH'] = path.resolve(__dirname, path.join('..','node_modules','ios-sim','build','release')) + ':' + process.env['PATH'];
    require('child_process').exec('which ios-sim', function(err, stdout, stderr) {
        if (err !== null) {
            console.error('****** ios-sim is not installed on path. `sudo npm install -g ios-sim` if you want this server to support emulator.');
        } else {
            console.info('ios-sim is installed on path at: %s', stdout);
        }
    });
};
 
function cdToAppDir(emulateRequest) {
    process.chdir(emulateRequest.appDir);
    return emulateRequest;
}
 
function cordovaEmulate(emulateRequest) {
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    var emulatorAppPath = util.quotesAroundIfNecessary(path.join(emulateRequest.appDir, 'platforms', 'ios', 'build', 'emulator', emulateRequest.appName + '.app'));
    exec('killall \'iPhone Simulator\'', function (error, stdout, stderr) {
        exec('ios-sim launch ' + emulatorAppPath + ' ' + iosSimTarget(emulateRequest.target) + ' --exit', function (error, stdout, stderr) {
            if (error !== null) {
                deferred.reject(error);
            } else {
                deferred.resolve();
            }
        });
    });
    return deferred.promise;
}
 
var iosSimTargets = {
    'iphone 4s': '--retina',
    'iphone 5': '--retina --tall',
    'iphone 5s': '--retina --tall --64bit',
    'iphone 6': '--devicetypeid com.apple.CoreSimulator.SimDeviceType.iPhone-6',
    'iphone 6 plus': '--devicetypeid com.apple.CoreSimulator.SimDeviceType.iPhone-6-Plus',
    'ipad 2': '--family ipad',
    'ipad air': '--family ipad --retina --64bit',
    'ipad retina': '--family ipad --retina'
};
 
function iosSimTarget(emulateRequestTarget) {
    emulateRequestTarget = emulateRequestTarget.toLowerCase();
    var iosSimTarget = iosSimTargets[emulateRequestTarget] || '--family iphone --retina';
    return iosSimTarget;
}

"use strict";
 
var util = require('./util'),
    CordovaConfig = require('./CordovaConfig'),
    path = require('path'),
    fs = require('fs'),
    pl = require('plist-with-patches');
 
var plist = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var templateContents = null;
 
plist.createEnterprisePlist = function(cordovaConfigOrPathToConfigXml, outFilePath) {
    var cfg = cordovaConfigOrPathToConfigXml;
    if (typeof cordovaConfigOrPathToConfigXml === 'string') {
        cfg = new CordovaConfig(cordovaConfigOrPathToConfigXml);
    }
    var id = cfg.id();
    var version = cfg.version();
    var name = cfg.name();
 
    var plistContents = getTemplateContents();
    plistContents = plistContents.replace('${BUNDLE_IDENTIFIER}', id);
    plistContents = plistContents.replace('${APPLICATION_VERSION}', version);
    plistContents = plistContents.replace('${DISPLAY_NAME}', name);
    util.writeFileContentsSync(outFilePath, plistContents);
    console.info('Created plist file %s from template with [%s, %s, %s]', outFilePath, id, version, name);
};
 
plist.updateAppBundleVersion = function(pathToAppPlist, buildNumber) {
    var plistInfo = pl.parseFileSync(pathToAppPlist);
    var version = plistInfo['CFBundleVersion'];
    version = version ? version + '.' + buildNumber : ''+buildNumber;
    plistInfo['CFBundleVersion'] = version;
    var updatedPlistContents = pl.build(plistInfo);
    updatedPlistContents = updatedPlistContents.replace(/<string>[\s\r\n]*<\/string>/g,'<string></string>');
    fs.writeFileSync(pathToAppPlist, updatedPlistContents, 'utf-8');
}
 
function getTemplateContents() {
    if (templateContents === null) {
        var templatePath = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'templates', 'EnterpriseApp.plist');
        templateContents = util.readFileContentsSync(templatePath, 'utf-8');
    }
    return templateContents;
}

/********************************************************

*   Copyright (C) Microsoft. All rights reserved.       *
*                                                       *

"use strict";
 
var fs = require('fs'),
    path = require('path'),
    util = require('./util');
 
var res = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var resources = null;
var defaultLang = 'en';
 
res.init = function(resourcesDir) {
    if (!resourcesDir) {
        resourcesDir = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'resources');
    }
    var supportedLanguages = fs.readdirSync(resourcesDir).filter(function(c) {
        return fs.existsSync(path.join(resourcesDir, c, 'resources.json'));
    });
    resources = {};
    supportedLanguages.forEach(function(l) {
        resources[l.toLowerCase()] = loadLanguage(resourcesDir, l);
    });
};
 
// Support acceptLangs as an array of strings like ['en-US', 'es'], 
// or a http request 'Accept-Language' format header like pl,fr-FR;q=0.3,en-US;q=0.1. For now we do not account for the quality (q) value
res.getString = function(requestOrAcceptLangs, id, optionalArgs) {
    if (resources === null) {
        throw new Error('Resources have not been loaded');
    }
 
    var lang = res.getBestLanguageMatchOrDefault(requestOrAcceptLangs);
    var s = resources[lang.toLowerCase()][id];
    if (!s) {
        return s;
    }
 
    var args = util.getOptionalArgsArrayFromFunctionCall(arguments, 2);
    if (args !== null) {
        for (var i=0; i < args.length; i++) {
            s = s.replace('{'+i+'}', args[i]);
        }
    }
    return s;
};
 
res.getResources = function(language) {
    return resources[language.toLowerCase()];
};
 
res.getBestLanguageMatchOrDefault = function(requestOrAcceptLangs) {
    var lang = bestLanguageMatch(requestOrAcceptLangs);
    if (lang === null || !resources[lang.toLowerCase()]) {
        lang = defaultLang;
    }
    return lang;
};
 
function bestLanguageMatch(requestOrAcceptLangs) {
    if (!requestOrAcceptLangs || requestOrAcceptLangs === null) {
        return null;
    }
    var acceptLangs = [];
    if (Array.isArray(requestOrAcceptLangs) || typeof requestOrAcceptLangs === 'string') {
        acceptLangs = requestOrAcceptLangs;
    } else if (requestOrAcceptLangs.headers) {
        acceptLangs = requestOrAcceptLangs.headers['accept-language'];
    } else {
        throw new Error('Unsupported type of argument for acceptLangs: ' + (typeof acceptLangs));
    }
    if (typeof acceptLangs === 'string') {
        acceptLangs = acceptLangs.split(',').map(function(lang) {
            return lang.split(';')[0];
        });
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(acceptLangs) || acceptLangs.length === 0) {
        return null;
    }
 
    var supportedLanguages = Object.keys(resources);
    var primaryLangMatch = null;
    for (var i=0; i < acceptLangs.length; i++) {
        var lang = acceptLangs[i].toLowerCase();
        if (supportedLanguages.indexOf(lang) !== -1) {
            // exact match on full language header, which could include the region (e.g. it-CH), return the match
            return lang;
        }
        var primaryLang = lang.split('-')[0];
        if (supportedLanguages.indexOf(primaryLang) !== -1) {
            // match on primary language (e.g. it from it-CH). Continue the loop so we don't prevent a possible exact match.
            primaryLangMatch = primaryLang;
        }
    }
 
    return primaryLangMatch;
}
 
function loadLanguage(resourcesDir, language) {
    var resourcesPath = path.join(resourcesDir, language, 'resources.json');
    console.info('Loading resources for language %s from %s', language, resourcesPath);
    return require(resourcesPath);
}

"use strict";
 
var express = require('express'),
    http = require('http'),
    https = require('https'),
    path = require('path'),
    fs = require('fs'),
    os = require('os'),
    Q = require('q'),
    rimraf = require('rimraf'),
    buildmgr = require('./buildManager'),
    resources = require('./resources'),
    certs = require('./certs'),
    util = require('./util'),
    runner = require('./appRunner');
 
var server = exports = module.exports = {};
var serverInstance;
var serverConf;
 
server.start = function(conf) {
 
    if (process.getuid() === 0) {
        console.warn(resources.getString(conf.get('lang'),"NotRunAsRoot"));
        process.exit(1);
    }
 
    var app = express();
    app.set('port', conf.get('port'));
    app.set('serverDir', conf.get('serverDir'));
    app.use(express.logger('dev'));
    app.use(express.errorHandler());
 
    // Initialize the build manager (after our app settings are all setup)
    buildmgr.init(conf);
 
    var onlyAuthorizedClientRequest = function(req, res, next) {
        if (!req.client.authorized) {
            res.send(401, resources.getString(req, 'UnauthorizedClientRequest'));
        } else {
            next();
        }
    };
 
    app.get('/', function(req, res) {
        res.send(200, resources.getString(req, 'IndexPageContent', app.get('port')));
    });
 
    // These routes are fully secured through client cert verification:
    if (util.argToBool(conf.get('secure')) === true) {
        app.all('/build/*', onlyAuthorizedClientRequest);
        app.all('/files', onlyAuthorizedClientRequest);
    }
    app.post('/build/tasks', submitNewBuild);
    app.get('/build/tasks/:id', getBuildStatus);
    app.get('/build/tasks/:id/log', getBuildLog);
    app.get('/build/tasks', getAllBuildStatus);
    app.get('/build/:id', getBuild);
    app.get('/build/:id/download', downloadBuild);
    app.get('/build/:id/emulate', emulateBuild);
    app.get('/build/:id/deploy', deployBuild);
    app.get('/build/:id/run', runBuild);
    app.get('/build/:id/debug', debugBuild);
    app.get('/debugPort', getDebugPort);
 
    app.get('/certs/:pin', downloadClientCerts);
    app.get('/resources/:lang', getResources);
 
    app.use('/files', express.directory(buildmgr.getBaseBuildDir()));
    app.use('/files', express.static(buildmgr.getBaseBuildDir()));
 
    return startupServer(conf, app).
            then(registerShutdownHooks).
            fail(function(err) {
                console.error(resources.getString(conf.get("lang"),"ServerStartFailed"), err);
                if (err.stack) {
                    console.error(err.stack);
                }
                throw err;
            });
};
 
server.stop = function(callback) {
    serverInstance.close(callback);
};
 
server.resetServerCert = function(conf) {
    return certs.resetServerCert(conf);
};
 
server.generateClientCert = function(conf) {
    return certs.generateClientCert(conf);
};
 
function startupServer(conf, app) {
    var isSsl = util.argToBool(conf.get('secure'));
    return (isSsl === true) ? startupHttpsServer(conf, app) : startupPlainHttpServer(conf, app);
}
 
function startupPlainHttpServer(conf, app) {
    return Q(http.createServer(app)).
            then(function(svr) {
                var deferred = Q.defer();
                svr.on('error', function (err) {
                    deferred.reject(friendlyServerListenError(err, conf));
                });
                svr.listen(app.get('port'), function() {
                    serverInstance = svr;
                    serverConf = conf;
                    console.log(resources.getString(conf.get("lang"),"InsecureServerStarted"), app.get('port'));
                    writePid();
                    deferred.resolve(svr);
                });
                return deferred.promise;
            });
}
 
function friendlyServerListenError(err, conf) {
    if (err.code == 'EADDRINUSE') {
        return resources.getString(conf.get("lang"),"ServerPortInUse", conf.get('port'));
    } else {
        return err;
    }
}
 
function writePid() {
    if (util.argToBool(serverConf.get('writePidToFile')) === true) {
        fs.writeFile(path.join(serverConf.get('serverDir'), "running_process_id"), process.pid);
    }
}
 
function startupHttpsServer(conf, app) {
    var generatedNewCerts = false;
    var generatedClientPin;
    return certs.initializeServerCerts(conf).
            then(function(certPaths) {
                if (certPaths.newCerts === true) {
                    generatedNewCerts = true;
                    conf.suppressVisualStudioMessage = true;
                    return certs.generateClientCert(conf).
                            then(function(pin) {
                                generatedClientPin = pin;
                                return certPaths;
                            });
                }
                return certPaths;
            }).
            then(function(certPaths) {
                var sslSettings = {
                    key: fs.readFileSync(certPaths.serverKeyPath),
                    cert: fs.readFileSync(certPaths.serverCertPath),
                    ca: fs.readFileSync(certPaths.caCertPath),
                    requestCert: true,
                    rejectUnauthorized: false
                };
                return https.createServer(sslSettings, app);
            }).
            then(function(svr) {
                var deferred = Q.defer();
                svr.on('error', function (err) {
                    if (generatedNewCerts === true) {
                        certs.removeAllCertsSync(conf);
                    }
                    deferred.reject(friendlyServerListenError(err, conf));
                });
                svr.listen(app.get('port'), function() {
                    serverInstance = svr;
                    serverConf = conf;
                    console.log(resources.getString(conf.get("lang"), "SecureServerStarted"), app.get('port'));
                    writePid();
                    deferred.resolve(svr);
                });
                return deferred.promise;
            });
}
function registerShutdownHooks() {
    // We should have serverConf defined at this point, but just in case fall back to english
    var lang = serverConf && serverConf.get('lang') || 'en';
    // It is strongly recommended in a NodeJs server to kill the process off on uncaughtException.
    process.on('uncaughtException', function (err) {
      console.error(resources.getString(lang, "UncaughtErrorShutdown") + err);
      console.error(err.stack);
      console.info(resources.getString(lang,"ServerShutdown"));
      buildmgr.shutdown();
      runner.shutdown();
      process.exit(1)
    });
 
    // Opportunity to clean up builds on exit
    var shutdown = function() {
        console.info(resources.getString(lang, "ServerShutdown"));
        buildmgr.shutdown();
        serverInstance.close();
        process.exit(0);
    };
    process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown);
    process.on('SIGINT', shutdown);
}
 
// Submits a new build task
function submitNewBuild(req, res) {
    buildmgr.submitNewBuild(req, function(err, buildInfo) {
        if (err) {
            res.set({'Content-Type': 'application/json'});
            res.send(400, {status: resources.getString(req, 'InvalidBuildRequest'), errors: err});
        } else {
            var contentLocation = ((util.argToBool(serverConf.get('secure')) === true) ? 'https://' : 'http://')  + 
                                    req.headers.host + '/build/tasks/' + buildInfo.buildNumber;
            res.set({
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Content-Location': contentLocation
            });
            res.json(202, buildInfo.localize(req));
        }
    });
}
 
// Queries on the status of all build tasks
function getAllBuildStatus(req, res) {
    var allBuildInfo = buildmgr.getAllBuildInfo();
    res.json(200, allBuildInfo);
}
 
// Queries on the status of a build task, used by a client to poll
function getBuildStatus(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// Retrieves log file for a build task, can be used by a client when build failed
function getBuildLog(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        res.set('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
        buildmgr.downloadBuildLog(req.params.id, res);
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// Gets a build.
function getBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
        return;
    }
    res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
}
 
// Emulates a build.
function emulateBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        buildmgr.emulateBuild(req.params.id, req.query.target, function(err, result) {
                if (err) {
                    res.send(404, err);
                } else {
                    res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
                }
            });
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// installs a build on a device
function deployBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        buildmgr.installBuild(req.params.id, function (err, result) {
            if (err) {
				if (err.reason) {
					res.send(404, resources.getString(req, err.reason));
				} else if (err.message) {
					res.send(404, err.message);
				} else {
					res.send(404, err);
				}
            } else {
                res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
            }
        });
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// runs a build on a device
function runBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        buildmgr.runBuild(req.params.id, function (err, result) {
            if (err) {
                res.send(404, err);
            } else {
                res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
            }
        });
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// debugs a build on a device
function debugBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo !== null) {
        buildmgr.debugBuild(req.params.id, function (err, result) {
            if (err) {
                res.send(404, resources.getString(req, err));
            } else {
                res.json(200, buildInfo.localize(req));
            }
        });
    } else {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
    }
}
 
// debugs a build on a device
function getDebugPort(req, res) {
    res.json(200, [{ 'webDebugPort' : buildmgr.getDebugPort() }]);
    
}
 
// Downloads a build as a zip file with .ipa and .plist file
function downloadBuild(req, res) {
    var buildInfo = buildmgr.getBuildInfo(req.params.id);
    if (buildInfo === null) {
        res.send(404, resources.getString(req, 'BuildNotFound', req.params.id));
        return;
    }
    buildmgr.downloadBuild(req.params.id, res, function(err, updatedBuildInfo) {
        if (err) {
            res.send(404, err);
        }
    });
}
 
// Returns the resources for the requested language
function getResources(req, res) {
    var lang = req.params.lang;
    var langResources = resources.getResources(lang);
    if (langResources === null) {
        res.send(404, resources.getString('NoResourcesForLanguage', lang));
    } else {
        res.send(200, langResources);
    }
}
 
// Downloads client SSL certs (pfx format) for pin specified in request
function downloadClientCerts(req, res) {
    certs.purgeExpiredPinBasedClientCertsSync(serverConf);
    var clientCertsDir = path.join(serverConf.get('serverDir'), 'certs', 'client');
 
    var pin = parseInt(req.params.pin);
    if (isNaN(pin)) {
        res.send(400, resources.getString('InvalidPIN'));
        return;
    }
 
    var pinDir = path.join(clientCertsDir, ''+pin);
    var pfx = path.join(pinDir, 'client.pfx');
    if (!fs.existsSync(pfx)) {
        res.send(404, resources.getString('ClientCertNotFoundForPIN'));
        return;
    }
 
    res.sendfile(pfx);
    rimraf(pinDir, function() {});
}
