"use strict";
 
var fs = require('fs'),
    path = require('path'),
    mkdirp = require('mkdirp'),
    rimraf = require('rimraf'),
    ncp = require('ncp'),
    semver = require('semver'),
    exec = require('child_process').exec,
    Q = require('q');
 
var util = exports = module.exports = {};
 
var CordovaCliSpecType = {
    Error: -1,
    Version: 0,
    URI: 1
}
 
util.createDirectoryIfNecessary = function (dir) {
    if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
        try {
            mkdirp.sync(dir);
            return true;
        } catch (err) {
            // if multiple msbuild processes are running on a first time solution build, another one might have created the basedir. check again.
            if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
                throw err;
            }
        }
    }
    return false;
};
 
util.readFileContentsSync = function (filename, encoding) {
    var contents = fs.readFileSync(filename, (encoding || 'utf-8'));
    if (contents) {
        contents = contents.replace(/^\uFEFF/, ''); //Windows is the BOM
    }
    return contents;
};
 
util.writeFileContentsSync = function (filename, contents, encoding) {
    fs.writeFileSync(filename, contents, encoding);
};
 
util.copyFileSync = function (from, to, encoding) {
    var contents = util.readFileContentsSync(from, encoding);
    util.writeFileContentsSync(to, contents, encoding);
};
 
// Recursively copy 'source' to 'target'
util.copyRecursive = function (source, target) {
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    var options = {};
    
    ncp(source, target, options, function (error) {
        if (error) {
            deferred.reject(new Error(error));
        } else {
            deferred.resolve();
        }
    });
    
    return deferred.promise;
};
 
var invalidAppNameChars = {
    34: '"',
    36: '$',
    38: '&',
    39: '/',
    60: '<',
    92: '\\'
};
 
util.isValidCordovaAppName = function (str) {
    for (var i = 0, n = str.length; i < n; i++) {
        var code = str.charCodeAt(i);
        if (code < 32 || invalidAppNameChars[code]) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
};
 
util.invalidAppNameCharacters = function () {
    var x = [];
    Object.keys(invalidAppNameChars).forEach(function (c) {
        x.push(invalidAppNameChars[c]);
    });
    return x;
};
 
util.getOptionalArgsArrayFromFunctionCall = function (functionArguments, startFrom) {
    if (functionArguments.length <= startFrom) {
        return null;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(functionArguments[startFrom])) {
        return functionArguments[startFrom];
    }
    return Array.prototype.slice.apply(functionArguments, [startFrom]);
};
 
util.quotesAroundIfNecessary = function quotesAroundIfNecessary(filename) {
    return (filename.indexOf(' ') > -1) ? '"' + filename + '"' : filename;
}
 
util.argToBool = function (input) {
    if (typeof input === 'string') {
        return input.toLowerCase() === 'true';
    }
    return !!input
}
 
util.cleanFolderOnFailure = function (path) {
    if (fs.existsSync(path)) {
        rimraf(path, function (error) {
            deferred.reject(error);
        });
    }
}
 
util.CloneGitRepo = function (gitUrl, cloneTargetPath) {
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    
    try {
        console.log('Installing Cordova tools for project from {0}. This could take a few minutes...', gitUrl);
        
        // Clone the GIT repository to the target path
        exec("git clone " + gitUrl + " " + cloneTargetPath, {}, function (error, stdout, stderr) {
            if (error) {
                console.warn(stdout);
                console.warn(stderr);
                util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cloneTargetPath);
                deferred.reject(new Error('GIT clone of ' + gitUrl + ' failed. Error: ' + error));
            } else {
                console.log('GIT clone of ' + gitUrl + ' completed.');
                deferred.resolve(true);
            }
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.log(error);
        util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cloneTargetPath);
        deferred.reject(new Error('GIT clone of ' + gitUrl + ' failed. Error: ' + error));
    }
    return deferred.promise;
}
 
util.getCliSpecType = function (cliVersion) {
    // The Cordova CLI specification in taco.json can either be a GIT url or an npm package version number
    var gitUrlRegex = new RegExp("^http(s?)\\:\/\/.*|.*\.git$");
    
    if (semver.valid(cliVersion) !== null) {
        return CordovaCliSpecType.Version;
    }
    
    if ((gitUrlRegex.exec(cliVersion)) !== null) {
        return CordovaCliSpecType.URI;
    }
    
    return CordovaCliSpecType.Error;
}
 
util.installCordovaFromNPM = function (cliVersion, cordovaCliTargetPath) {
    var cordova;
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    try {
        mkdirp.sync(cordovaCliTargetPath);
        console.log('Installing Cordova tools {0} for project from NPM. This could take a few minutes...', 'cordova' + '@' + cliVersion);
        
        exec("npm install " + "cordova" + "@" + cliVersion, { cwd: cordovaCliTargetPath }, function (error, stdout, stderr) {
            if (error) {
                console.warn(stdout);
                console.warn(stderr);
                util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                deferred.reject(new Error('npm install error: cordova' + '@' + cliVersion));
            } else {
                console.log('npm install of cordova@' + cliVersion + 'from npm completed.');
                cordova = require(path.join(cordovaCliTargetPath, 'cordova'));
                deferred.resolve(cordova);
            }
        });
    } catch (err) {
        console.log(err);
        util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath);
        deferred.reject(new Error('npm install error cordova@' + cliVersion));
    }
    return deferred.promise;
}
 
util.lazyloadCordovaModule = function (cliVersion, serverDir) {
    var cordova;
    var cordovaCliTargetPath;
    var npmCommand;
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    
    var cordovaModulesPath = path.join(serverDir, 'node_modules', 'cordova');
    switch (util.getCliSpecType(cliVersion)) {
        case CordovaCliSpecType.Version:
            {
                npmCommand = "npm install " + "cordova" + "@" + cliVersion;
                cordovaCliTargetPath = path.join(cordovaModulesPath, cliVersion, 'node_modules');
                var statusFilePath = path.join(cordovaCliTargetPath, '..', 'Installing.tmp');
                if (!fs.existsSync(path.join(cordovaCliTargetPath, 'cordova', 'package.json')) || fs.existsSync(statusFilePath)) {
                    // Delete the target path if it already exists and create an empty folder
                    if (fs.existsSync(cordovaCliTargetPath)) {
                        rimraf.sync(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                    }
                    mkdirp.sync(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                    fs.closeSync(fs.openSync(statusFilePath, 'w'));
                    util.installCordovaFromNPM(cliVersion, cordovaCliTargetPath).then(function (cordova) {
                        rimraf(statusFilePath, function (error) {
                            if (error) {
                                deferred.reject(error);
                            }
                        });
                        deferred.resolve(cordova);
                    }).catch(function (error) {
                        deferred.reject(error);
                    });
                }
                else {
                    try {
                        cordova = require(path.join(cordovaCliTargetPath, 'cordova'));
                        deferred.resolve(cordova);
                    }
                    catch (e) {
                        util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                        deferred.reject(new Error('ERROR: A module failed to load.'));
                    }
                }
            }
            break;
        case CordovaCliSpecType.URI:
            {
                var localRepoName = cliVersion;
                var decodedURI = decodeURIComponent(cliVersion);
                cordovaCliTargetPath = path.join(cordovaModulesPath, localRepoName, 'cordova');
                var statusFilePath = path.resolve(cordovaCliTargetPath, '..', 'Installing.tmp');
                
                // If the repo is available locally and is not malformed, use it
                // Else, clone the repository and install the module
                if (fs.existsSync(cordovaCliTargetPath) && !fs.existsSync(statusFilePath)) {
                    console.log('Cordova tools from GIT repository' + decodedURI + 'already installed');
                    try {
                        cordova = require(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                        deferred.resolve(cordova);
                    }
                    catch (e) {
                        util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath, deferred);
                        deferred.reject(new Error('ERROR: A module failed to load.'));
                    }
                }
                else {
                    // Delete the target path if it already exists and create an empty folder
                    if (fs.existsSync(cordovaCliTargetPath)) {
                        rimraf.sync(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                    }
                    mkdirp.sync(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                    fs.closeSync(fs.openSync(statusFilePath, 'w'));
                    util.CloneGitRepo(decodedURI, cordovaCliTargetPath).then(function () {
                        exec("npm install", { cwd: cordovaCliTargetPath }, function (error, stdout, stderr) {
                            if (error) {
                                console.warn(stdout);
                                console.warn(stderr);
                                console.log(error);
                                util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath);
                                deferred.reject(new Error('npm install error: cordova' + '@' + decodedURI));
                            } else {
                                console.log(stdout);
                                console.log('npm install of cordova from' + decodedURI + 'completed.');
                                try {
                                    rimraf(statusFilePath, function (error) {
                                        if (error) {
                                            deferred.reject(error);
                                        }
                                    });
                                    cordova = require(path.join(cordovaCliTargetPath, 'cordova'));
                                    deferred.resolve(cordova);
                                }
                                catch (e) {
                                    util.cleanFolderOnFailure(cordovaCliTargetPath, deferred);
                                    deferred.reject(new Error('ERROR: A module failed to load.'));
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }).done();
                }
            }
            break;
        case CordovaCliSpecType.Error:
        default:
            {
                deferred.reject(new Error('Unknown Cordova CLI version'));
            }
    }
    return deferred.promise;
}
